# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Produce artifacts** — Express all code changes as **unified diffs** in your output artifact (e.g., `fix_patch` fields in review.json, or a standalone `solution.patch` file). Do NOT edit source files directly — there are none in your workspace.

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-cross-k8s-arch-001: Kubernetes CRD Lifecycle (Cross-Repo)

## Task

Trace how a Custom Resource Definition (CRD) flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem: from CRD type definitions and validation, through etcd storage and the dynamic HTTP handler, to the generated client, informers, listers, and the dynamic client. Map the complete lifecycle across four logical sub-projects within the Kubernetes monorepo.

## Context

- **Repository**: kubernetes/kubernetes (Go, ~2.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding (cross-repo)
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/, staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/, staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/, staging/src/k8s.io/api/

## Architecture Overview

Kubernetes uses a staging directory structure where four logically separate projects coexist in one monorepo:

1. **apiextensions-apiserver** — CRD type definitions, validation, etcd storage, dynamic HTTP handler
2. **client-go** — Generated typed clients, informers, listers, and the dynamic client
3. **apimachinery** — Runtime scheme, GVK/GVR types, ObjectMeta, Unstructured representation
4. **api** — Internal hub types and group registration

## Requirements

1. Trace the CRD type definition layer: internal hub types, external v1 types, and Scheme registration
2. Map the server-side lifecycle: validation, etcd storage, and the dynamic customresource_handler
3. Trace the client-side access layer: typed clientset, SharedIndexInformer, Lister, and DynamicClient
4. Identify the foundational types in apimachinery that everything depends on: Scheme, GVK/GVR, TypeMeta/ObjectMeta, Unstructured

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Foundation: apimachinery types (Scheme, GVK, ObjectMeta, Unstructured)
2. Type definitions: apiextensions types (internal hub + external v1 + registration)
3. Server-side: validation -> etcd storage -> HTTP handler
4. Client-side: typed client -> informer -> lister -> dynamic client
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Cross-project dependency flow
- How CRD types bridge the four sub-projects
- The role of Scheme and GVK in type registration
- How Unstructured enables dynamic custom resource access
- The checkpoint between server-side storage and client-side informer caching]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary of the CRD lifecycle across the K8s ecosystem]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find files across ALL four sub-projects?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct cross-project dependency chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you identify how the sub-projects integrate?

76-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the CRD lifecycle across the Kubernetes ecosystem. Let me verify the solution is complete by reviewing what I've delivered:

## Analysis Complete ✓

I've traced the CRD lifecycle across all four sub-projects and written the analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md`. Here's what the analysis covers:

### **Files Examined** (Cross all 4 sub-projects)
- **apiextensions-apiserver**: Type definitions (internal hub + v1), HTTP handler, storage, validation
- **client-go**: Dynamic client, informers, listers, REST client foundation
- **apimachinery**: Scheme, GVK/GVR, ObjectMeta, Unstructured, serialization
- **api**: Type registration infrastructure

### **Dependency Chain** (4 Layers)
1. **Foundation**: Scheme registry, GVK/GVR identifiers, ObjectMeta, Unstructured type, codec system
2. **Type Definitions**: Internal hub types + external v1 types with SchemeBuilder pattern registration
3. **Server-Side**: Validation against CRD schema → etcd storage via generic REST → dynamic HTTP handler
4. **Client-Side**: RESTClient → Typed client (for CRDs) → Dynamic client (for CRs) → Informers → Listers

### **Key Architectural Insights**
- **Unstructured Type** is the bridge: enables schema-less storage and client access without type registration
- **Scheme Registry** ties typed and untyped access together while remaining independent
- **HTTP Handler** dynamically creates `/apis/{group}/{version}/{resource}` endpoints from CRDs
- **Informers** establish ListWatch connections to cache CRs locally with event-driven updates
- **GVK vs GVR**: GVK identifies data format, GVR identifies API endpoint—the Scheme provides conversion

The analysis demonstrates how a CRD flows from definition → validation → storage → HTTP endpoint → client-side cach

  "content": "# CRD Lifecycle Analysis: Cross-Kubernetes Ecosystem\n\n## Files Examined\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver: Type Definitions & Server-Side Lifecycle\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go` \u2014 Internal hub type definitions for CustomResourceDefinition, CustomResourceDefinitionSpec, CustomResourceValidation\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/register.go` \u2014 External v1 API types and Scheme registration for CustomResourceDefinition and ConversionReview\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go` \u2014 v1-versioned type definitions with versioning logic\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` \u2014 Dynamic HTTP handler that processes CustomResource requests at runtime\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` \u2014 Storage backend implementation using etcd via generic REST storage\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/strategy.go` \u2014 Storage strategy for validation, field handling, and etcd predicates\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/strategy.go` \u2014 CRD-specific storage strategy for the CRD resource itself\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/crdserverscheme/crdserverscheme.go` \u2014 Scheme for serving CRD types with unstructured representation\n\n### client-go: Client-Side Access Layer\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` \u2014 DynamicClient wrapping rest.Interface for schema-less access to any resource\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` \u2014 DynamicSharedInformerFactory and DynamicInformer for watching CRs with ListWatch pattern\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/informers/generic.go` \u2014 GenericInformer interface and genericInformer implementation wrapping SharedIndexInformer and cache.GenericLister\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` \u2014 Generic listers for filtering cached CRs from the informer cache\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/typed/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` \u2014 Typed client for CustomResourceDefinition resources (for managing CRDs themselves)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/rest/client.go` \u2014 Base RESTClient providing HTTP semantics for all client operations\n\n### apimachinery: Foundation Types & Runtime System\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go` \u2014 Scheme type registry mapping GVK \u2194 Go struct types, manages type conversion and serialization\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/schema/group_version.go` \u2014 GroupVersionKind and GroupVersionResource definitions for identifying resource types\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go` \u2014 Unstructured type (map[string]interface{}) enabling schema-less object representation\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go` \u2014 TypeMeta and ObjectMeta with standard API fields (apiVersion, kind, name, namespace, etc.)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/serializer/` \u2014 Codec factories for encoding/decoding objects in JSON, CBOR, protobuf\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go` \u2014 ObjectTyper, Encoder, Decoder interfaces defining the type system boundaries\n\n### api: Type Registration & Hub Types\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/` \u2014 Contains no CRD types directly, but core/v1 defines ObjectMeta and standard API group types\n- Type registration happens through SchemeBuilder pattern (AddToScheme functions)\n- Serves as the authoritative source for API group structures across the ecosystem\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### 1. **Foundation: apimachinery Types**\n\nThe entire CRD ecosystem is built on foundational types defined in apimachinery:\n\n#### Scheme (runtime.Scheme)\n- Central registry maintaining bidirectional mappings:\n  - `GVK \u2192 reflect.Type` (what Go type represents this Kind?)\n  - `reflect.Type \u2192 []GVK` (what versions does this type have?)\n- Manages serialization codecs for objects\n- Enables runtime type discovery and conversion\n- Example: `scheme.AddKnownTypes(GroupVersion, &CustomResourceDefinition{})`\n\n#### GroupVersionKind (GVK) & GroupVersionResource (GVR)\n- **GVK**: Identifies the *data format* (apiVersion + kind) \u2192 `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1 CustomResourceDefinition`\n- **GVR**: Identifies the *API endpoint* (group + version + plural resource name) \u2192 `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1/customresourcedefinitions`\n- Schema provides conversion: `GVK.GroupVersion().WithResource(resource)` \u2192 `GVR`\n\n#### ObjectMeta & TypeMeta\n- **TypeMeta**: Contains `apiVersion` and `kind` fields\n- **ObjectMeta**: Contains standard metadata (name, namespace, labels, annotations, uid, resourceVersion, etc.)\n- All Kubernetes objects embed both via composition\n\n#### Unstructured Type\n- `map[string]interface{}` wrapper enabling schema-less representation\n- Implements `runtime.Object`, `metav1.Object`, `metav1.ListInterface`\n- Key for dynamic clients: they work with Unstructured, not typed structs\n- Serialization: JSON \u2192 map unmarshaling, map \u2192 JSON marshaling\n\n---\n\n### 2. **Type Definitions: apiextensions-apiserver Types**\n\nCRD type definitions are split across internal (hub) and versioned (external) representations:\n\n#### Internal Hub Types\n- **Location**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`\n- **Purpose**: The canonical representation used internally for conversion and validation\n- **Key Types**:\n  - `CustomResourceDefinition`: Spec contains group, names, scope, validation schema, versions\n  - `CustomResourceDefinitionSpec`: Describes what a custom resource looks like\n  - `CustomResourceValidation`: JSONSchemaProps defining structural schema for CRs\n  - `CustomResourceDefinitionStatus`: Conditions tracking CRD establishment, acceptance, etc.\n- **Registration**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` adds these to internal GroupVersion\n\n#### External v1 Types\n- **Location**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`\n- **Purpose**: User-facing API surface with versioning guarantees\n- **Registration**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/register.go` registers to SchemeGroupVersion\n- **SchemeBuilder Pattern**:\n  ```go\n  var (\n    SchemeBuilder      = runtime.NewSchemeBuilder(addKnownTypes, addDefaultingFuncs)\n    localSchemeBuilder = &SchemeBuilder\n    AddToScheme        = localSchemeBuilder.AddToScheme\n  )\n\n  func addKnownTypes(scheme *runtime.Scheme) error {\n    scheme.AddKnownTypes(SchemeGroupVersion,\n      &CustomResourceDefinition{},\n      &CustomResourceDefinitionList{},\n      &ConversionReview{},\n    )\n    metav1.AddToGroupVersion(scheme, SchemeGroupVersion)\n    return nil\n  }\n  ```\n\n#### Scheme Integration Points\n1. apiextensions-apiserver initializes a scheme in `crdserverscheme.go`\n2. Typed client (client-go) has its own scheme registration for CRDs\n3. Dynamic client uses unstructured scheme, bypassing typed registration\n\n---\n\n### 3. **Server-Side Lifecycle: Validation \u2192 Storage \u2192 HTTP Handler**\n\n#### Validation Layer\n- **Location**: `pkg/apiserver/validation/` and `pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/strategy.go`\n- **Process**:\n  1. CRD Spec contains JSONSchemaProps defining CustomResource validation rules\n  2. On CR Create/Update, apiextensions-apiserver validates against the CRD's schema\n  3. Validation is structural: object properties, type checking, required fields\n  4. Conversion webhooks (in ConversionStrategy) transform CRs between versions\n\n#### etcd Storage Layer\n- **Location**: `pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` and `strategy.go`\n- **Pattern**: Generic etcd backend provided by apiserver framework\n- **Key Mechanism**:\n  ```go\n  // In etcd.go\n  type REST struct {\n    *genericregistry.Store  // Wraps generic etcd storage\n  }\n\n  // Storage key path in etcd: /customresources/{group}/{version}/{kind}/{namespace}/{name}\n  ```\n- **Storage Strategy**: Implements predicates for field/label filtering, name validation\n- **Serialization**: Objects stored as JSON in etcd, deserialized to Unstructured on retrieval\n\n#### Dynamic HTTP Handler\n- **Location**: `pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`\n- **Purpose**: Serves `/apis/{group}/{version}/{resource}` endpoints for all CRs\n- **Architecture**:\n  1. `crdHandler` filters HTTP requests by path and routes to appropriate storage\n  2. For each CRD, maintains a `crdStorage` map with a REST storage instance\n  3. On CRD change (add/update/delete), handler rebuilds storage map\n  4. Handles all CRUD operations: Get, List, Watch, Create, Update, Delete, Patch\n- **Key Pattern**: Handler is registered as a filter, never collides with explicitly registered endpoints\n- **Serialization**: Handles content negotiation (JSON, CBOR, protobuf) via NegotiatedSerializer\n\n#### Discovery & OpenAPI\n- **Endpoint**: `/openapi/v3` provides OpenAPI schema for all resources including CRs\n- **Generated**: `pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go` watches CRDs and updates OpenAPI spec\n- **Discovery**: `/api` and `/apis/{group}` endpoints list available resources\n\n---\n\n### 4. **Client-Side Access Layer: Typed Client \u2192 Informer \u2192 Lister \u2192 Dynamic Client**\n\n#### RESTClient Foundation\n- **Location**: `client-go/rest/client.go`\n- **Role**: Low-level HTTP client\n- **Responsibilities**:\n  - Request building (URL, headers, query params)\n  - Authentication (kubeconfig, serviceaccount tokens)\n  - Transport handling (TLS, keep-alive)\n  - Response unmarshaling\n\n#### Typed Client (for CRD Management)\n- **Generated Location**: `client-go/kubernetes/typed/apiextensions/v1/`\n- **Purpose**: Typed access to CustomResourceDefinition resources themselves\n- **Example**: `clientset.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().Create(crd)`\n- **Type Safety**: Uses Go structs (CustomResourceDefinition) with compile-time checking\n- **Scheme Usage**: Depends on apimachinery's Scheme for type registration\n\n#### Dynamic Client (for Custom Resources)\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/simple.go`\n- **Wraps**: `rest.Interface` (RESTClient)\n- **Uses**: `Unstructured` type for all objects\n- **Key Properties**:\n  - Schema-less: No compile-time type registration required\n  - GVR-based: Identifies resources by GroupVersionResource, not Scheme\n  - Works immediately with CRs without code generation\n- **Example**:\n  ```go\n  client := dynamic.NewForConfig(config)\n  resource := schema.GroupVersionResource{\n    Group: \"example.com\",\n    Version: \"v1\",\n    Resource: \"widgets\",\n  }\n  widgets := client.Resource(resource).Namespace(\"default\")\n  ```\n\n#### Informers & Listers (Client-Side Cache)\n- **Location**: `client-go/informers/` and `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/`\n- **Purpose**: Local in-memory cache of resources with watch support\n\n##### SharedIndexInformer Flow\n1. **ListWatch Construction** (`dynamicinformer/informer.go:150-176`):\n   - ListFunc: `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).List(ctx, options)`\n   - WatchFunc: `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).Watch(ctx, options)`\n   - These funcs delegate to DynamicClient \u2192 RESTClient\n\n2. **Caching** (`tools/cache/shared_informer.go`):\n   - Stores objects in thread-safe Indexers\n   - Listwatch periodically lists all objects (resync), watches for changes\n   - Objects cached as Unstructured\n\n3. **Event Handling**:\n   - Informer maintains a queue of Add/Update/Delete events\n   - Calls registered eventhandlers for each event\n   - Indexers updated in response\n\n##### Lister Pattern\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/`\n- **Purpose**: Query interface over the informer cache\n- **Operations**:\n  - `List(selector)`: Get all objects matching label selector from cache\n  - `Get(name)`: Get single object from cache\n  - `ByNamespace(ns)`: Restrict to specific namespace\n- **Type**: `cache.GenericLister` interface works with Unstructured objects\n\n##### GenericInformer Interface\n- **Location**: `client-go/informers/generic.go`\n- **Definition**:\n  ```go\n  type GenericInformer interface {\n    Informer() cache.SharedIndexInformer\n    Lister() cache.GenericLister\n  }\n  ```\n- **Usage**: Abstracts over typed and dynamic informers with same interface\n\n#### DynamicSharedInformerFactory\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go`\n- **Purpose**: Multiplexes informers for multiple CRDs\n- **Key Method**: `ForResource(gvr)` \u2192 `GenericInformer` for that GVR\n- **Lifecycle**:\n  1. Create factory: `NewDynamicSharedInformerFactory(client, resync)`\n  2. Get informer: `factory.ForResource(gvr).Informer()`\n  3. Start: `factory.Start(stopCh)` launches watchers in goroutines\n  4. Wait sync: `factory.WaitForCacheSync(stopCh)` ensures all caches populated\n  5. Query: `factory.ForResource(gvr).Lister().List(selector)`\n\n---\n\n## Analysis: How the Sub-Projects Integrate\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery (Foundation)\n    \u2193 (defines core types)\n    \u251c\u2192 Scheme, GVK/GVR, ObjectMeta, Unstructured, Codec interfaces\n\napiextensions-apiserver (Server-Side)\n    \u2193 (depends on apimachinery)\n    \u251c\u2192 Extends Scheme with CustomResourceDefinition types\n    \u251c\u2192 Uses Unstructured for storing arbitrary CRs\n    \u251c\u2192 Validates CRs against CRD schemas\n    \u251c\u2192 Stores in etcd using generic REST storage\n    \u2514\u2192 Serves HTTP endpoints for CRUD + Watch\n\nclient-go (Client-Side)\n    \u2193 (depends on apimachinery + apiextensions for CRD types)\n    \u251c\u2192 Provides RESTClient for HTTP requests\n    \u251c\u2192 Typed client for CustomResourceDefinition management\n    \u251c\u2192 Dynamic client for CustomResource access (Unstructured)\n    \u251c\u2192 Informers for caching with ListWatch\n    \u2514\u2192 Listers for querying cache\n\napi (Hub Types)\n    \u2193 (authoritative definitions)\n    \u2514\u2192 Provides standard ObjectMeta, TypeMeta, etc.\n```\n\n### The Bridge: Unstructured Representation\n\nThe critical innovation enabling the CRD architecture:\n1. **On Server**: CRDs define validation via JSONSchemaProps, but CRs stored as Unstructured JSON in etcd\n2. **On Wire**: Objects transmitted as JSON with apiVersion/kind in TypeMeta\n3. **On Client**: DynamicClient receives Unstructured objects, can query/manipulate without schema knowledge\n4. **Checkpoint**: Validation happens server-side before storage, client-side type checking is optional\n\n### Scheme Registration Patterns\n\n**Typed CRD Client**:\n```go\n// In apiextensions-apiserver and client-go\nscheme := runtime.NewScheme()\napiextensionsv1.AddToScheme(scheme)  // Registers CustomResourceDefinition, ConversionReview types\n```\n\n**Dynamic Client**:\n```go\n// In client-go/dynamic\nconfig := ConfigFor(inConfig)\nconfig.NegotiatedSerializer = newBasicNegotiatedSerializer()  // Unstructured codec only\n// No Scheme registration needed!\n```\n\n### The Informer Checkpoint\n\nWhen a DynamicInformer watches a CRD's CRs:\n1. **Server-Side**: customresource_handler watches etcd, returns Unstructured objects\n2. **Over Wire**: HTTP/Watch stream delivers serialized Unstructured (as JSON)\n3. **Client-Side**: DynamicClient deserializes to Unstructured\n4. **In Cache**: Informer's Indexers store Unstructured objects\n5. **Query Time**: Lister returns Unstructured from cache\n\nNo type conversion happens; objects remain Unstructured throughout the pipeline.\n\n### Why Four Sub-Projects?\n\n1. **apimachinery**: Stable foundation used by all Kubernetes code; changes rarely break compatibility\n2. **apiextensions-apiserver**: Can evolve CRD API without breaking apimachinery consumers\n3. **client-go**: Isolated client library; can be vendored independently with different versions than apiserver\n4. **api**: Core and extension API definitions; separates type definitions from implementation\n\nEach project has its own versioning, release cycle, and import constraints. This modularity allows:\n- Users can update client-go independently from their cluster version\n- New CRD features don't require updating all consumers\n- Clear separation of concerns: definitions (api) vs runtime (apiextensions) vs client libraries (client-go)\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nA Custom Resource Definition flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem as follows:\n\n**Server-side**: A CRD type definition (stored as a CustomResourceDefinition object) is validated, stored in etcd, and served via the dynamic HTTP handler which creates a REST endpoint for custom resources. The endpoint validates CRs against the CRD's schema and stores them as Unstructured JSON objects in etcd.\n\n**Client-side**: Clients access custom resources via the DynamicClient, which performs HTTP requests to the CRD-provided endpoints. A DynamicSharedInformerFactory establishes ListWatch connections, caching Unstructured objects locally and maintaining an in-memory index. Listers query this cache using the GenericInformer interface, enabling operator code to efficiently watch and react to CR changes without compile-time knowledge of the resource type.\n\n**Cross-cutting**: The Scheme registry in apimachinery ties typed and untyped clients together, while GroupVersionKind/GroupVersionResource identifiers enable routing and discovery. The Unstructured type allows the entire pipeline to work with schema-less objects, making CRDs extensible without requiring code generation for each new resource type.\n",

`staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/scheme.go` \u2014 Scheme type registry mapping GVK \u2194 Go struct types, manages type conversion and serialization\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/schema/group_version.go` \u2014 GroupVersionKind and GroupVersionResource definitions for identifying resource types\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured/unstructured.go` \u2014 Unstructured type (map[string]interface{}) enabling schema-less object representation\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go` \u2014 TypeMeta and ObjectMeta with standard API fields (apiVersion, kind, name, namespace, etc.)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/serializer/` \u2014 Codec factories for encoding/decoding objects in JSON, CBOR, protobuf\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go` \u2014 ObjectTyper, Encoder, Decoder interfaces defining the type system boundaries\n\n### api: Type Registration & Hub Types\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/` \u2014 Contains no CRD types directly, but core/v1 defines ObjectMeta and standard API group types\n- Type registration happens through SchemeBuilder pattern (AddToScheme functions)\n- Serves as the authoritative source for API group structures across the ecosystem\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### 1. **Foundation: apimachinery Types**\n\nThe entire CRD ecosystem is built on foundational types defined in apimachinery:\n\n#### Scheme (runtime.Scheme)\n- Central registry maintaining bidirectional mappings:\n  - `GVK \u2192 reflect.Type` (what Go type represents this Kind?)\n  - `reflect.Type \u2192 []GVK` (what versions does this type have?)\n- Manages serialization codecs for objects\n- Enables runtime type discovery and conversion\n- Example: `scheme.AddKnownTypes(GroupVersion, &CustomResourceDefinition{})`\n\n#### GroupVersionKind (GVK) & GroupVersionResource (GVR)\n- **GVK**: Identifies the *data format* (apiVersion + kind) \u2192 `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1 CustomResourceDefinition`\n- **GVR**: Identifies the *API endpoint* (group + version + plural resource name) \u2192 `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1/customresourcedefinitions`\n- Schema provides conversion: `GVK.GroupVersion().WithResource(resource)` \u2192 `GVR`\n\n#### ObjectMeta & TypeMeta\n- **TypeMeta**: Contains `apiVersion` and `kind` fields\n- **ObjectMeta**: Contains standard metadata (name, namespace, labels, annotations, uid, resourceVersion, etc.)\n- All Kubernetes objects embed both via composition\n\n#### Unstructured Type\n- `map[string]interface{}` wrapper enabling schema-less representation\n- Implements `runtime.Object`, `metav1.Object`, `metav1.ListInterface`\n- Key for dynamic clients: they work with Unstructured, not typed structs\n- Serialization: JSON \u2192 map unmarshaling, map \u2192 JSON marshaling\n\n---\n\n### 2. **Type Definitions: apiextensions-apiserver Types**\n\nCRD type definitions are split across internal (hub) and versioned (external) representations:\n\n#### Internal Hub Types\n- **Location**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go`\n- **Purpose**: The canonical representation used internally for conversion and validation\n- **Key Types**:\n  - `CustomResourceDefinition`: Spec contains group, names, scope, validation schema, versions\n  - `CustomResourceDefinitionSpec`: Describes what a custom resource looks like\n  - `CustomResourceValidation`: JSONSchemaProps defining structural schema for CRs\n  - `CustomResourceDefinitionStatus`: Conditions tracking CRD establishment, acceptance, etc.\n- **Registration**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` adds these to internal GroupVersion\n\n#### External v1 Types\n- **Location**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go`\n- **Purpose**: User-facing API surface with versioning guarantees\n- **Registration**: `pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/register.go` registers to SchemeGroupVersion\n- **SchemeBuilder Pattern**:\n  ```go\n  var (\n    SchemeBuilder      = runtime.NewSchemeBuilder(addKnownTypes, addDefaultingFuncs)\n    localSchemeBuilder = &SchemeBuilder\n    AddToScheme        = localSchemeBuilder.AddToScheme\n  )\n\n  func addKnownTypes(scheme *runtime.Scheme) error {\n    scheme.AddKnownTypes(SchemeGroupVersion,\n      &CustomResourceDefinition{},\n      &CustomResourceDefinitionList{},\n      &ConversionReview{},\n    )\n    metav1.AddToGroupVersion(scheme, SchemeGroupVersion)\n    return nil\n  }\n  ```\n\n#### Scheme Integration Points\n1. apiextensions-apiserver initializes a scheme in `crdserverscheme.go`\n2. Typed client (client-go) has its own scheme registration for CRDs\n3. Dynamic client uses unstructured scheme, bypassing typed registration\n\n---\n\n### 3. **Server-Side Lifecycle: Validation \u2192 Storage \u2192 HTTP Handler**\n\n#### Validation Layer\n- **Location**: `pkg/apiserver/validation/` and `pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/strategy.go`\n- **Process**:\n  1. CRD Spec contains JSONSchemaProps defining CustomResource validation rules\n  2. On CR Create/Update, apiextensions-apiserver validates against the CRD's schema\n  3. Validation is structural: object properties, type checking, required fields\n  4. Conversion webhooks (in ConversionStrategy) transform CRs between versions\n\n#### etcd Storage Layer\n- **Location**: `pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` and `strategy.go`\n- **Pattern**: Generic etcd backend provided by apiserver framework\n- **Key Mechanism**:\n  ```go\n  // In etcd.go\n  type REST struct {\n    *genericregistry.Store  // Wraps generic etcd storage\n  }\n\n  // Storage key path in etcd: /customresources/{group}/{version}/{kind}/{namespace}/{name}\n  ```\n- **Storage Strategy**: Implements predicates for field/label filtering, name validation\n- **Serialization**: Objects stored as JSON in etcd, deserialized to Unstructured on retrieval\n\n#### Dynamic HTTP Handler\n- **Location**: `pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`\n- **Purpose**: Serves `/apis/{group}/{version}/{resource}` endpoints for all CRs\n- **Architecture**:\n  1. `crdHandler` filters HTTP requests by path and routes to appropriate storage\n  2. For each CRD, maintains a `crdStorage` map with a REST storage instance\n  3. On CRD change (add/update/delete), handler rebuilds storage map\n  4. Handles all CRUD operations: Get, List, Watch, Create, Update, Delete, Patch\n- **Key Pattern**: Handler is registered as a filter, never collides with explicitly registered endpoints\n- **Serialization**: Handles content negotiation (JSON, CBOR, protobuf) via NegotiatedSerializer\n\n#### Discovery & OpenAPI\n- **Endpoint**: `/openapi/v3` provides OpenAPI schema for all resources including CRs\n- **Generated**: `pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go` watches CRDs and updates OpenAPI spec\n- **Discovery**: `/api` and `/apis/{group}` endpoints list available resources\n\n---\n\n### 4. **Client-Side Access Layer: Typed Client \u2192 Informer \u2192 Lister \u2192 Dynamic Client**\n\n#### RESTClient Foundation\n- **Location**: `client-go/rest/client.go`\n- **Role**: Low-level HTTP client\n- **Responsibilities**:\n  - Request building (URL, headers, query params)\n  - Authentication (kubeconfig, serviceaccount tokens)\n  - Transport handling (TLS, keep-alive)\n  - Response unmarshaling\n\n#### Typed Client (for CRD Management)\n- **Generated Location**: `client-go/kubernetes/typed/apiextensions/v1/`\n- **Purpose**: Typed access to CustomResourceDefinition resources themselves\n- **Example**: `clientset.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().Create(crd)`\n- **Type Safety**: Uses Go structs (CustomResourceDefinition) with compile-time checking\n- **Scheme Usage**: Depends on apimachinery's Scheme for type registration\n\n#### Dynamic Client (for Custom Resources)\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/simple.go`\n- **Wraps**: `rest.Interface` (RESTClient)\n- **Uses**: `Unstructured` type for all objects\n- **Key Properties**:\n  - Schema-less: No compile-time type registration required\n  - GVR-based: Identifies resources by GroupVersionResource, not Scheme\n  - Works immediately with CRs without code generation\n- **Example**:\n  ```go\n  client := dynamic.NewForConfig(config)\n  resource := schema.GroupVersionResource{\n    Group: \"example.com\",\n    Version: \"v1\",\n    Resource: \"widgets\",\n  }\n  widgets := client.Resource(resource).Namespace(\"default\")\n  ```\n\n#### Informers & Listers (Client-Side Cache)\n- **Location**: `client-go/informers/` and `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/`\n- **Purpose**: Local in-memory cache of resources with watch support\n\n##### SharedIndexInformer Flow\n1. **ListWatch Construction** (`dynamicinformer/informer.go:150-176`):\n   - ListFunc: `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).List(ctx, options)`\n   - WatchFunc: `client.Resource(gvr).Namespace(ns).Watch(ctx, options)`\n   - These funcs delegate to DynamicClient \u2192 RESTClient\n\n2. **Caching** (`tools/cache/shared_informer.go`):\n   - Stores objects in thread-safe Indexers\n   - Listwatch periodically lists all objects (resync), watches for changes\n   - Objects cached as Unstructured\n\n3. **Event Handling**:\n   - Informer maintains a queue of Add/Update/Delete events\n   - Calls registered eventhandlers for each event\n   - Indexers updated in response\n\n##### Lister Pattern\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/`\n- **Purpose**: Query interface over the informer cache\n- **Operations**:\n  - `List(selector)`: Get all objects matching label selector from cache\n  - `Get(name)`: Get single object from cache\n  - `ByNamespace(ns)`: Restrict to specific namespace\n- **Type**: `cache.GenericLister` interface works with Unstructured objects\n\n##### GenericInformer Interface\n- **Location**: `client-go/informers/generic.go`\n- **Definition**:\n  ```go\n  type GenericInformer interface {\n    Informer() cache.SharedIndexInformer\n    Lister() cache.GenericLister\n  }\n  ```\n- **Usage**: Abstracts over typed and dynamic informers with same interface\n\n#### DynamicSharedInformerFactory\n- **Location**: `client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go`\n- **Purpose**: Multiplexes informers for multiple CRDs\n- **Key Method**: `ForResource(gvr)` \u2192 `GenericInformer` for that GVR\n- **Lifecycle**:\n  1. Create factory: `NewDynamicSharedInformerFactory(client, resync)`\n  2. Get informer: `factory.ForResource(gvr).Informer()`\n  3. Start: `factory.Start(stopCh)` launches watchers in goroutines\n  4. Wait sync: `factory.WaitForCacheSync(stopCh)` ensures all caches populated\n  5. Query: `factory.ForResource(gvr).Lister().List(selector)`\n\n---\n\n## Analysis: How the Sub-Projects Integrate\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery (Foundation)\n    \u2193 (defines core types)\n    \u251c\u2192 Scheme, GVK/GVR, ObjectMeta, Unstructured, Codec interfaces\n\napiextensions-apiserver (Server-Side)\n    \u2193 (depends on apimachinery)\n    \u251c\u2192 Extends Scheme with CustomResourceDefinition types\n    \u251c\u2192 Uses Unstructured for storing arbitrary CRs\n    \u251c\u2192 Validates CRs against CRD schemas\n    \u251c\u2192 Stores in etcd using generic REST storage\n    \u2514\u2192 Serves HTTP endpoints for CRUD + Watch\n\nclient-go (Client-Side)\n    \u2193 (depends on apimachinery + apiextensions for CRD types)\n    \u251c\u2192 Provides RESTClient for HTTP requests\n    \u251c\u2192 Typed client for CustomResourceDefinition management\n    \u251c\u2192 Dynamic client for CustomResource access (Unstructured)\n    \u251c\u2192 Informers for caching with ListWatch\n    \u2514\u2192 Listers for querying cache\n\napi (Hub Types)\n    \u2193 (authoritative definitions)\n    \u2514\u2192 Provides standard ObjectMeta, TypeMeta, etc.\n```\n\n### The Bridge: Unstructured Representation\n\nThe critical innovation enabling the CRD architecture:\n1. **On Server**: CRDs define validation via JSONSchemaProps, but CRs stored as Unstructured JSON in etcd\n2. **On Wire**: Objects transmitted as JSON with apiVersion/kind in TypeMeta\n3. **On Client**: DynamicClient receives Unstructured objects, can query/manipulate without schema knowledge\n4. **Checkpoint**: Validation happens server-side before storage, client-side type checking is optional\n\n### Scheme Registration Patterns\n\n**Typed CRD Client**:\n```go\n// In apiextensions-apiserver and client-go\nscheme := runtime.NewScheme()\napiextensionsv1.AddToScheme(scheme)  // Registers CustomResourceDefinition, ConversionReview types\n```\n\n**Dynamic Client**:\n```go\n// In client-go/dynamic\nconfig := ConfigFor(inConfig)\nconfig.NegotiatedSerializer = newBasicNegotiatedSerializer()  // Unstructured codec only\n// No Scheme registration needed!\n```\n\n### The Informer Checkpoint\n\nWhen a DynamicInformer watches a CRD's CRs:\n1. **Server-Side**: customresource_handler watches etcd, returns Unstructured objects\n2. **Over Wire**: HTTP/Watch stream delivers serialized Unstructured (as JSON)\n3. **Client-Side**: DynamicClient deserializes to Unstructured\n4. **In Cache**: Informer's Indexers store Unstructured objects\n5. **Query Time**: Lister returns Unstructured from cache\n\nNo type conversion happens; objects remain Unstructured throughout the pipeline.\n\n### Why Four Sub-Projects?\n\n1. **apimachinery**: Stable foundation used by all Kubernetes code; changes rarely break compatibility\n2. **apiextensions-apiserver**: Can evolve CRD API without breaking apimachinery consumers\n3. **client-go**: Isolated client library; can be vendored independently with different versions than apiserver\n4. **api**: Core and extension API definitions; separates type definitions from implementation\n\nEach project has its own versioning, release cycle, and import constraints. This modularity allows:\n- Users can update client-go independently from their cluster version\n- New CRD features don't require updating all consumers\n- Clear separation of concerns: definitions (api) vs runtime (apiextensions) vs client libraries (client-go)\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nA Custom Resource Definition flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem as follows:\n\n**Server-side**: A CRD type definition (stored as a CustomResourceDefinition object) is validated, stored in etcd, and served via the dynamic HTTP handler which creates a REST endpoint for custom resources. The endpoint validates CRs against the CRD's schema and stores them as Unstructured JSON objects in etcd.\n\n**Client-side**: Clients access custom resources via the DynamicClient, which performs HTTP requests to the CRD-provided endpoints. A DynamicSharedInformerFactory establishes ListWatch connections, caching Unstructured objects locally and maintaining an in-memory index. Listers query this cache using the GenericInformer interface, enabling operator code to efficiently watch and react to CR changes without compile-time knowledge of the resource type.\n\n**Cross-cutting**: The Scheme registry in apimachinery ties typed and untyped clients together, while GroupVersionKind/GroupVersionResource identifiers enable routing and discovery. The Unstructured type allows the entire pipeline to work with schema-less objects, making CRDs extensible without requiring code generation for each new resource type.\n",
